(100 / (1 + rs))\n    17→    return df\n    18→\n    19→\n    20→def add_macd(\n    21→    df: pd.DataFrame,\n    22→    fast: int = 12,\n    23→    slow: int = 26,\n    24→    signal: int = 9,\n    25→    column: str = \"close\"\n    26→) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    27→    \"\"\"Add MACD and signal line.\"\"\"\n    28→    ema_fast = df[column].ewm(span=fast, adjust=False).mean()\n    29→    ema_slow = df[column].ewm(span=slow, adjust=False).mean()\n    30→    df[\"macd\"] = ema_fast - ema_slow\n    31→    df[\"macd_signal\"] = df[\"macd\"].ewm(span=signal, adjust=False).mean()\n    32→    df[\"macd_hist\"] = df[\"macd\"] - df[\"macd_signal\"]\n    33→    return df\n    34→\n    35→\n    36→def add_bollinger_bands(\n    37→    df: pd.DataFrame,\n    38→    period: int = 20,\n    39→    std: float = 2,\n    40→    column: str = \"close\"\n    41→) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    42→    \"\"\"Add Bollinger Bands.\"\"\"\n    43→    rolling_mean = df[column].rolling(window=period).mean()\n    44→    rolling_std = df[column].rolling(window=period).std()\n    45→    df[\"bb_middle\"] = rolling_mean\n    46→    df[\"bb_upper\"] = rolling_mean + (rolling_std * std)\n    47→    df[\"bb_lower\"] = rolling_mean - ema_slow\n    df[\"macd_signal\"] = df[\"macd\"].ewm(span=signal, adjust=False).mean()\n    df[\"macd_hist\"] = df[\"macd\"] - df[\"macd_signal\"]\n    return df\n\n\ndef add_bollinger_bands(\n    df: pd.DataFrame,\n    period: int = 20,\n    std: float = 2,\n    column: str = \"close\"\n) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"Add Bollinger Bands.\"\"\"\n    rolling_mean = df[column].rolling(window=period).mean()\n    rolling_std = df[column].rolling(window=period).std()\n    df[\"bb_middle\"] = rolling_mean\n    df[\"bb_upper\"] = rolling_mean + (rolling_std * std)\n    df[\"bb_lower\"] = rolling_mean - (rolling_std * std)\n    df[\"bb_width\"] = (df[\"bb_upper\"] - df[\"bb_lower\"]) / rolling_mean\n    df[\"bb_position\"] = (df[column] - df[\"bb_lower\"]) / (df[\"bb_upper\"] - df[\"bb_lower\"] + 1e-10)\n    return df\n\n\ndef add_atr(\n    df: pd.DataFrame,\n    period: int = 14,\n    high_col: str = \"high\",\n    low_col: str = \"low\",\n    close_col: str = \"close\"\n) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"Add Average True Range.\"\"\"\n    high_low = df[high_col] - df[low_col]\n    high_close = abs(df[high_col] - df[close_col].shift())\n    low_close = abs(df[low_col] - df[close_col].shift())\n\n    ranges = pd.concat([high_low, high_close, low_close], axis=1)\n    true_range = ranges.max(axis=1)\n    df[\"atr\"] = true_range.rolling(window=period).mean()\n    df[\"atr_ratio\"] = df[\"atr\"] / df[close_col]\n    return df\n\n\ndef add_momentum(df: pd.DataFrame, periods: List[int] = [5, 10, 20]) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"Add momentum features (rate of change).\"\"\"\n    for period in periods:\n        df[f\"mom_{period}\"] = df[\"close\"].pct_change(period)\n    return df\n\n\ndef add_volume_features(\n    df: pd.DataFrame,\n    ma_periods: List[int] = [5, 10, 20]\n) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"Add volume-based features.\"\"\"\n    for period in ma_periods:\n        df[f\"volume_ma_{period}\"] = df[\"volume\"].rolling(window=period).mean()\n        df[f\"volume_ratio_{period}\"] = df[\"volume\"] / (df[f\"volume_ma_{period}\"] + 1e-10)\n\n    # Volume spike detection\n    df[\"volume_z\"] = (df[\"volume\"] - df[\"volume\"].rolling(20).mean()) / (df[\"volume\"].rolling(20).std() + 1e-10)\n\n    return df\n\n\ndef add_technical_indicators(df: pd.DataFrame, config=None) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"\n    Add all technical indicators to DataFrame.\n\n    Args:\n        df: DataFrame with OHLCV columns\n        config: FeatureConfig (optional, uses defaults if None)\n    \"\"\"\n    df = df.copy()\n\n    # Add all indicators\n    df = add_rsi(df)\n    df = add_macd(df)\n    df = add_bollinger_bands(df)\n    df = add_atr(df)\n    df = add_momentum(df, periods=[1, 3, 5, 10, 15, 20])\n    df = add_volume_features(df, ma_periods=[5, 10, 20])\n\n    # Additional price-derived features\n    df[\"price_range\"] = (df[\"high\"] - df[\"low\"]) / df[\"close\"]\n    df[\"close_open_ratio\"] = df[\"close\"] / df[\"open\"]\n    df[\"high_low_ratio\"] = df[\"high\"] / df[\"low\"]\n\n    return df\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":91,"oldLines":6,"newStart":91,"newLines":20,"lines":["     return df"," "," ","+def add_time_features(df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:","+    \"\"\"Add cyclical time-of-day and day-of-week features (crypto has strong session patterns).\"\"\"","+    if \"open_time\" not in df.columns:","+        return df","+    dt = pd.to_datetime(df[\"open_time\"])","+    hour = dt.dt.hour + dt.dt.minute / 60.0","+    dow = dt.dt.dayofweek.astype(float)","+    df[\"hour_sin\"] = np.sin(2 * np.pi * hour / 24.0)","+    df[\"hour_cos\"] = np.cos(2 * np.pi * hour / 24.0)","+    df[\"dow_sin\"] = np.sin(2 * np.pi * dow / 7.0)","+    df[\"dow_cos\"] = np.cos(2 * np.pi * dow / 7.0)","+    return df","+","+"," def add_technical_indicators(df: pd.DataFrame, config=None) -> pd.DataFrame:","     \"\"\"","     Add all technical indicators to DataFrame."]},{"oldStart":114,"oldLines":4,"newStart":128,"newLines":7,"lines":["     df[\"close_open_ratio\"] = df[\"close\"] / df[\"open\"]","     df[\"high_low_ratio\"] = df[\"high\"] / df[\"low\"]"," ","+    # Cyclical time features (session patterns: Asia/EU/US opens)","+    df = add_time_features(df)","+","     return df"]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

(100 / (1 + rs))\n    return df\n\n\ndef add_macd(\n    df: pd.DataFrame,\n    fast: int = 12,\n    slow: int = 26,\n    signal: int = 9,\n    column: str = \"close\"\n) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"Add MACD and signal line.\"\"\"\n    ema_fast = df[column].ewm(span=fast, adjust=False).mean()\n    ema_slow = df[column].ewm(span=slow, adjust=False).mean()\n    df[\"macd\"] = ema_fast - ema_slow\n    df[\"macd_signal\"] = df[\"macd\"].ewm(span=signal, adjust=False).mean()\n    df[\"macd_hist\"] = df[\"macd\"] - df[\"macd_signal\"]\n    return df\n\n\ndef add_bollinger_bands(\n    df: pd.DataFrame,\n    period: int = 20,\n    std: float = 2,\n    column: str = \"close\"\n) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"Add Bollinger Bands.\"\"\"\n    rolling_mean = df[column].rolling(window=period).mean()\n    rolling_std = df[column].rolling(window=period).std()\n    df[\"bb_middle\"] = rolling_mean\n    df[\"bb_upper\"] = rolling_mean + (rolling_std * std)\n    df[\"bb_lower\"] = rolling_mean - (rolling_std * std)\n    df[\"bb_width\"] = (df[\"bb_upper\"] - df[\"bb_lower\"]) / rolling_mean\n    df[\"bb_position\"] = (df[column] - df[\"bb_lower\"]) / (df[\"bb_upper\"] - df[\"bb_lower\"] + 1e-10)\n    return df\n\n\ndef add_atr(\n    df: pd.DataFrame,\n    period: int = 14,\n    high_col: str = \"high\",\n    low_col: str = \"low\",\n    close_col: str = \"close\"\n) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"Add Average True Range.\"\"\"\n    high_low = df[high_col] - df[low_col]\n    high_close = abs(df[high_col] - df[close_col].shift())\n    low_close = abs(df[low_col] - df[close_col].shift())\n\n    ranges = pd.concat([high_low, high_close, low_close], axis=1)\n    true_range = ranges.max(axis=1)\n    df[\"atr\"] = true_range.rolling(window=period).mean()\n    df[\"atr_ratio\"] = df[\"atr\"] / df[close_col]\n    return df\n\n\ndef add_momentum(df: pd.DataFrame, periods: List[int] = [5, 10, 20]) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"Add momentum features (rate of change).\"\"\"\n    for period in periods:\n        df[f\"mom_{period}\"] = df[\"close\"].pct_change(period)\n    return df\n\n\ndef add_volume_features(\n    df: pd.DataFrame,\n    ma_periods: List[int] = [5, 10, 20]\n) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"Add volume-based features.\"\"\"\n    for period in ma_periods:\n        df[f\"volume_ma_{period}\"] = df[\"volume\"].rolling(window=period).mean()\n        df[f\"volume_ratio_{period}\"] = df[\"volume\"] / (df[f\"volume_ma_{period}\"] + 1e-10)\n\n    # Volume spike detection\n    df[\"volume_z\"] = (df[\"volume\"] - df[\"volume\"].rolling(20).mean()) / (df[\"volume\"].rolling(20).std() + 1e-10)\n\n    return df\n\n\ndef add_time_features(df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"Add cyclical time-of-day and day-of-week features (crypto has strong session patterns).\"\"\"\n    if \"open_time\" not in df.columns:\n        return df\n    dt = pd.to_datetime(df[\"open_time\"])\n    hour = dt.dt.hour + dt.dt.minute / 60.0\n    dow = dt.dt.dayofweek.astype(float)\n    df[\"hour_sin\"] = np.sin(2 * np.pi * hour / 24.0)\n    df[\"hour_cos\"] = np.cos(2 * np.pi * hour / 24.0)\n    df[\"dow_sin\"] = np.sin(2 * np.pi * dow / 7.0)\n    df[\"dow_cos\"] = np.cos(2 * np.pi * dow / 7.0)\n    return df\n\n\ndef add_technical_indicators(df: pd.DataFrame, config=None) -> pd.DataFrame:\n    \"\"\"\n    Add all technical indicators to DataFrame.\n\n    Args:\n        df: DataFrame with OHLCV columns\n        config: FeatureConfig (optional, uses defaults if None)\n    \"\"\"\n    df = df.copy()\n\n    # Add all indicators\n    df = add_rsi(df)\n    df = add_macd(df)\n    df = add_bollinger_bands(df)\n    df = add_atr(df)\n    df = add_momentum(df, periods=[1, 3, 5, 10, 15, 20])\n    df = add_volume_features(df, ma_periods=[5, 10, 20])\n\n    # Additional price-derived features\n    df[\"price_range\"] = (df[\"high\"] - df[\"low\"]) / df[\"close\"]\n    df[\"close_open_ratio\"] = df[\"close\"] / df[\"open\"]\n    df[\"high_low_ratio\"] = df[\"high\"] / df[\"low\"]\n\n    # Cyclical time features (session patterns: Asia/EU/US opens)\n    df = add_time_features(df)\n\n    return df\n","structuredPatch":[{"oldStart":91,"oldLines":20,"newStart":91,"newLines":6,"lines":["     return df"," "," ","-def add_time_features(df: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:","-    \"\"\"Add cyclical time-of-day and day-of-week features (crypto has strong session patterns).\"\"\"","-    if \"open_time\" not in df.columns:","-        return df","-    dt = pd.to_datetime(df[\"open_time\"])","-    hour = dt.dt.hour + dt.dt.minute / 60.0","-    dow = dt.dt.dayofweek.astype(float)","-    df[\"hour_sin\"] = np.sin(2 * np.pi * hour / 24.0)","-    df[\"hour_cos\"] = np.cos(2 * np.pi * hour / 24.0)","-    df[\"dow_sin\"] = np.sin(2 * np.pi * dow / 7.0)","-    df[\"dow_cos\"] = np.cos(2 * np.pi * dow / 7.0)","-    return df","-","-"," def add_technical_indicators(df: pd.DataFrame, config=None) -> pd.DataFrame:","     \"\"\"","     Add all technical indicators to DataFrame."]},{"oldStart":128,"oldLines":7,"newStart":114,"newLines":4,"lines":["     df[\"close_open_ratio\"] = df[\"close\"] / df[\"open\"]","     df[\"high_low_ratio\"] = df[\"high\"] / df[\"low\"]"," ","-    # Cyclical time features (session patterns: Asia/EU/US opens)","-    df = add_time_features(df)","-","     return df"]}],"userModified":false,"replaceAll":false}}

Metrics\n            accuracy = (pred == y_valid).mean()\n            all_metrics.append({\n                \"accuracy\": accuracy,\n                \"n_samples\": len(X_valid),\n                \"fold\": len(all_metrics)\n            })\n\n        if not all_metrics:\n            return {\"accuracy\": 0.0, \"n_folds\": 0}\n\n        # # Evaluate all individuals\n   178→            for i, ind in enumerate(pop.individuals):\n   179→                try:\n   180→                    print(f\"    Training individual                    pred = ind.model.predict(X_train, threshold=0.5)\n   184→                    accuracy = (pred == y_train).mean()\n   185→\n   186→                    # Simple fitness based on                pop.evolve()\n   197→\n   198→            best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n   199→            print(f\"    Best fitness: {best.fitness:.4f} (model={best.model_type})\", flush=True)\n   200→\n train_df: pd.DataFrame, valid_df: pd.DataFrame) -> Optional[Dict]:\n   220→        \"\"\"Run a single fold of walk-forward validation. Returns metrics dict or None.\"\"\"\n   221→        X_train = train_df[self.feature_names]\n   222→        y_train = train_df[\"target\"]\n   223→        X_valid = valid_df[self.feature_names]\n   224→        y_valid = valid_df[\"target\"]\n   225→        valid_ohlc = valid_df[['close', 'high', 'low']]\n   226→        close_prices = valid_df[\"close\"]\n   227→\n   228→        # Train fresh population on this fold's training data\n   229→        pop = Population(\n   230→            population_size=ModelConfig.POPULATION_SIZE,\n   231→            model_types=ModelConfig.MODEL_TYPES,\n   232→            mutation_rate=ModelConfig.MUTATION_RATE,\n   233→            crossover_rate=ModelConfig.CROSSOVER_RATE,\n   234→            elitism_count=ModelConfig.ELITISM_COUNT\n   235→        )\n   236→        pop.initialize(input_dim=X_train.shape[1], feature_names=self.feature_names)\n   237→\n   238→        for gen in range(ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION):\n   239→            for ind in pop.individuals:\n   240→                try:\n   241→                    ind.model.fit(X_train, y_train)\n   242→                    pred = ind.model.predict(X_train, threshold=0.5)\n   243→                    ind.fitness = (pred == y_train).mean()\n   244→                except Exception as e:\n   245→                    print(f\"    Training error: {e}\", flush=True)\n   246→                    ind.fitness = -1000.0\n   247→            if gen < ModelConfig.GENERATIONS_PER_ITERATION - 1:\n   248→                pop.evolve()\n   249→            best = pop.get_best(1)[0]\n   250→            print(f\"    Gen {gen+1}: best_train_fitness={best.fitness:.4f} ({best.model_type})\", flush=True)\n   251→\n   252→        # Re-score on validation set using profit_factor\n   253→        for i, ind in enumerate(pop.individuals):\n   254→            if ind.fitness is None or ind.fitness <= -1000:\n   255→                continue\n   256→            try:\n   257→                pred_valid = ind.model.predict(X_valid, threshold=0.5)\n   258→                if isinstance(pred_valid, np.ndarray):\n   259→                    pred_valid = pd.Series(pred_valid, index=X_valid.index)\n   260→                signals_ind = pred_valid.reindex(close_prices.index).fillna(-1).astype(int)\n   261→                self.trader.run(signals_ind, valid_ohlc)\n   262→                ind.fitness = self.trader.metrics.get('profit_factor', 0.0)\n   263→                ind.validation_metrics = self.trader.metrics\n   264→                print(f\"  Model {i+1}: profit_factor={ind.fitness:.4f}\", flush=True)\n   265→            except Exception as e:\n   266→                print(f\"  Rescoring error: {e}\", flush=True)\n   267→                ind.fitness = -1000.0\n   268→\n   269→        top_models = pop.get_diverse_best(n=5)\n   270→        self._log_feature_importances(top_models[0] if top_models else None)\n   271→\n   272→        # Determine how many non-overlapping folds fit (up to 3)\n   314→        n_folds = 1\n   315→        if total_rows >= 2 * val_rows + ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   316→            n_folds = 2\n   317→        if total_rows >= 3 * val_rows + ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   318→            n_folds = 3\n   319→\n   320→        fold_metrics = []\n   321→        for fold_idx in range(n_folds):\n   322→            # fold_idx=0 (earlier), fold_idx=1 (most recent)\n   323→            valid_end = total_rows - (n_folds - 1 - fold_idx) * val_rows\n   324→            valid_start = valid_end - val_rows\n   325→\n   326→            if valid_start < ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   327→                print(f\"Fold {fold_idx+1}: insufficient train samples, skipping.\", flush=True)\n   328→                continue\n   329→\n   330→            valid_df = df_sorted.iloc[valid_start:valid_end].copy()\n   331→            train_df = df_sorted.iloc[:valid_start].copy()\n   332→\n   333→            if len(train_df) > ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n   334→                train_df = train_df.tail(ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES).copy()\n   335→\n   336→            print(f\"\\nFold {fold_idx+1}/{n_folds}: train={len(train_df)}, valid={len(valid_df)}\", flush=True)\n   337→\n   338→            m = self._run_fold(train_df, valid_df)\n   339→            if m:\n   340→                fold_metrics.append(m)\n   341→\n   342→        if not fold_metrics:\n   343→            return {\"accuracy\": 0.0, \"bets_per_month\": 0.0, \"n_folds\": 0}\n   344→\n   345→        n = len(fold_metrics)\n   346→        total_trades = sum(m.get('n_trades', 0) for m in fold_metrics)\n   347→\n   348→        if total_trades == 0:\n   349→            combined = fold_metrics[-1].copy()\n   350→            combined[\"n_folds\"] = n\n   351→            return combined\n   352→\n   353→        # Aggregate: weighted accuracy by n_trades, average everything else\n   354→        accuracy = sum(m['accuracy'] * m.get('n_trades', 1) for m in fold_metrics) / total_trades\n   355→        combined = {\n   356→            \"accuracy\": accuracy,\n   357→            \"bets_per_month\": sum(m.get('bets_per_month', 0) for m in fold_metrics) / n,\n   358→            \"sharpe\": sum(m.get('sharpe', 0) for m in fold_metrics) / n,\n   359→            \"profit_factor\": sum(m.get('profit_factor', 0) for m in fold_metrics) / n,\n   360→            \"total_return\": sum(m.get('total_return', 0) for m in fold_metrics),\n   361→            \"max_drawdown\": max(m.get('max_drawdown', 0) for m in fold_metrics),\n   362→            \"n_trades\": total_trades,\n   363→            \"n_folds\": n,\n   364→        }\n   365→\n   366→        print(f\"\\nMulti-fold combined ({n} folds): accuracy={combined['accuracy']:.4f}, \"\n   367→              f\"bets/month={combined['bets_per_month']:.2f}, Sharpe={combined['sharpe']:.3f}, \"\n   368→              f\"total_return={combined['total_return']:.4f}, trades={total_trades}\", flush=True)\n   369→        return combined\n   370→\n   371→    def train_best_models(\n   372→        self,\n   373→        df: pd.DataFrame,\n   374→        population: Population,\n   375→        horizon_data: dict = None\n   376→    ):\n   377→        \"\"\"\n   378→        Train the best models on full recent data and optionally train horizon ensembles.\n   379→        \"\"\"\n   380→        print(\"Training best models on full data...\", flush=True)\n   381→\n   382→        # Returns metrics dict or None.\"\"\"\n        X_train = train_df[self.feature_names]\n        y_train = train_df[\"target\"]\n        X_valid = valid_df[self.feature_names]\n        y_valid = valid_df[\"target\"]\n        valid_ohlc = valid_df[['close', 'high', 'low']]\n        close_prices = valid_df[\"close\"]\n\n        # Determine how many non-overlapping folds fit (up to 3)\n        n_folds = 1\n        if total_rows >= 2 * val_rows + ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n            n_folds = 2\n        if total_rows >= 3 * val_rows + ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n            n_folds = 3\n\n        fold_metrics = []\n        for fold_idx in range(n_folds):\n            # fold_idx=0 (earlier), fold_idx=1 (most recent)\n            valid_end = total_rows - (n_folds - 1 - fold_idx) * val_rows\n            valid_start = valid_end - val_rows\n\n            if valid_start < ValidationConfig.MIN_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n                print(f\"Fold {fold_idx+1}: insufficient train samples, skipping.\", flush=True)\n                continue\n\n            valid_df = df_sorted.iloc[valid_start:valid_end].copy()\n            train_df = df_sorted.iloc[:valid_start].copy()\n\n            if len(train_df) > ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES:\n                train_df = train_df.tail(ModelConfig.MAX_TRAIN_SAMPLES).copy()\n\n            print(f\"\\nFold {fold_idx+1}/{n_folds}: train={len(train_df)}, valid={len(valid_df)}\", flush=True)\n\n            m = self._run_fold(train_df, valid_df)\n            if m:\n                fold_metrics.append(m)\n\n        if not fold_metrics:\n            return {\"accuracy\": 0.0, \"bets_per_month\": 0.0, \"n_folds\": 0}\n\n        n = len(fold_metrics)\n        total_trades = sum(m.get('n_trades', 0) for m in fold_metrics)\n\n        if total_trades == 0:\n            combined = fold_metrics[-1].copy()\n            combined[\"n_folds\"] = n\n            return combined\n\n        # _crossover(self, parent1: Individual, parent2: Individual) -> Individual:\n        \"\"\"Crossover between two parents (blend or swap).\"\"\"\n        if random.random() > self.crossover_rate:\n            return parent1\n\n        # Simple parameter averaging or swap for same model type\n        if parent1.model_type != parent2.model_type:\n            return parent1\n\n        child_params =
